name:Aâ€nâ€oâ€nâ€yâ€mâ€oâ€uâ€sâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Premier Single Room - River-View (Floor heating)
info:Stayed in May 2024

posted:Posted May 24, 2024
msg:Service: The hotel service is very good, especially Xiaoman, No. 007, who is very considerate. He helps with luggage and sends a travel guide. If you have any questions, you can ask him for help at any time, and he will solve them quickly and effectively.

Environment: The hotel is in a good location. It takes 5 minutes to walk to the east gate of Fanjing Mountain through the wind and rain bridge inside the hotel. In the lake view room you can see the clear Black River flowing slowly in the room, and it feels like being in a paradise with the sound of gurgling water and birds.

It is a 20-minute drive from the hotel to Yunshe Village, where you can eat local Tujia specialties and appreciate the Tujia customs.

It is also a 5-minute drive from the hotel to Zhaisha Dong Village. The village is not big, so you can also visit it when you are free. There are also bonfire parties on weekends.

Hygiene: The room is clean and tidy

Facilities: The hotel decoration style is standard, and the room area is OK. It is recommended to improve some details, such as hair dryers, towels and bath towels, which are too old.
There are many B&Bs and hotels around, and Qixi Resort Hotel has the best location. If the room supplies are improved, it will be better.

Since most of the guests staying here are those who get up early to climb Mount Fanjing, breakfast is basically over at 9:30. If you want to have breakfast, it is recommended to go earlier so that there are more varieties.

posted:Posted July 3, 2023
msg:Built against the mountain, it is inevitable that there will be a lot of humidity and mosquitoes.
Be sure to close the doors and windows in time. The quilts and sheets were all damp when you checked in, and you had to turn on the air conditioner to dehumidify it for a few hours in advance to get it back to normal. Breakfast is generally a filling stomach.
It is really very convenient to go to the scenic spot. Go out the back door of the hotel and cross the wind and rain bridge. After a few minutes, you will walk through the parking lot of the scenic spot and you will arrive at the gate.
It is recommended to stay, but the house price in summer is too high.
